<pictures>None<//pictures>< text>
Moderate-to-challenging hike up for first timers/inexperienced hikers as it is relatively steep in spots - total elevation gain just over 600 feet within the 1.7 round trip. The 5-stars is easily earned by the incredible scenery and views on the way up, fully appreciated at the very top of the rock with complete view of the lake. Prepare for a bit of a scramble to physically get onto the rock - look for a rope to assist with the climb up and down.<//text>

<rating>5< /rating>< Text>
Our go to restaurant when we need a chile relleno fix. The menu has many authentic and unusual choices. Someday we may try them but we can't seem to move past the rellenos.
They serve a little pot of hot bean dip with the pre-dinner chips and delicious salsa. We drive 50 miles to eat here at least once a month.
It's an easy 10 mile drive from Interstate 5. Take the Gustine exit. If you are a fan of authentic Mexican food, you will enjoy it.< /Text>

<response>{'time': 1580588315784, 'text': 'I understand how upsetting the sudden loss of your rabbit, Barnabus, is to you. I am deeply saddened by this as well, and offer my condolences to you and your wife, Anastassia. Rabbits and other defined ‚Äúprey‚Äù species are considered ‚Äúdelicate‚Äù animals as they have evolved a known reaction to fearful or stressful situations. Many veterinarians will not treat them because of this internal biological response, that can lead to an unforeseeable collapse and/or death. This flooding of ‚Äúflight or fight‚Äù sympathetic autonomic nervous system hormones, like epinephrine, can lead to cardiac abnormalities or other acute failures. Rabbits do require calm, careful approaches to examining and treating them. Because Barnabus was somewhat stressed from the exam, I tried to let him calm down in his kennel for several minutes. Because of your observation of a dark (presumed) urine, a urinalysis was recommended and authorized. He was carefully bundled in a towel to hopefully keep calm, secure, and to protect from bucking. After the procedure, we attempted to rewrap him and return him. Unfortunately, he leapt out of the bundle, and while trying to catch him before harm could come to him, he seemed to suffer the ‚Äúprey syndrome‚Äù. Despite our attempts to immediately treat him for this medical event, we were not successful. Please know there was not any inappropriate or negligent action. I am distressed this occurred and am sorry. These unpredictable events are heartbreaking for everyone involved. We try very hard to lower risk factors leading to this known, albeit horrifying, syndrome. Again, I am very sorry for your anguish and beyond saddened for your loss of your family member.'}</response>< gmapID>

I found this place on yelp, looking for a local deli. My partner had a craving for an egg salad with swiss, and I was on a mission to satisfy. Their location is almost hidden at the base of the towering bank buildings on Sunset. Though their giant red flags that read "Reggie's" seem like they would be adequate markers, (for an observant fella like myself), I noticed them waving high in the air on my way out of the sandwich shop. Anyhow, blah blah blah get to the point. Best egg salad sandwich we ever had. We've been 4 times in the last month or so and can't seem to veer away from the same order. Someday, I look forward to exploring their extensive menu :]
p.s. : their chocolate chip and snickerdoodle cookies are amazing AND the coleslaw is delicious. I'd bet you would not be disappointed with their non egg salad items. Ciao< /Text>

<user_id>111786517743281339317<//user_id><Rating>5<//Rating><time>1448096079529</time><text>When I think of Reggie's Deli & Caf√©, I'm immediately reminded of Cheers or the Central Perk from Friends. A place that gives off good vibes, friendly atmosphere, and an overall welcoming energy. It's no wonder that Reggie's has a near perfect 5-star rating! We were greeted warmly by Reggie himself as we walked through the doors, and all the workers and staff were incredibly friendly on a late Sunday morning.

Reggie's specializes in sandwiches, although the juices and gelato seem to come highly recommended. There's also wraps, salads, and breakfast sandwiches as well. They also offer a lunch special where you get half of a sandwich or wrap with a pint of soup or a salad for $8.95. My friend and I decided to just order two sandwiches and split it 50/50 so that we'd be able to try two sandwiches in one visit.

Food: We actually ordered Chicken Pesto panini and the Turkey Pesto panini, but when our orders came out, we realized that we didn't get the Turkey Pesto but the turkey club instead. It wasn't a big deal and luckily the sandwich was quite tasty. Both sandwiches came with a cucumber salad and a pickle. Out of the two sandwiches, I would say that I enjoyed the chicken pesto much more, just because it had pesto in it. With all the ingredients on toasted bread, the combination worked really well. The turkey breast wasn't too spectacular - I think better than your average Subway sandwich, but nothing amazing. It was loaded with fresh ingredients and tasted good, but I was a bit disappointed that we didn't get the turkey pesto like we had originally wanted.

Ambience: There's plenty of tables outside the deli as well as a few inside if you want to avoid the ever-changing LA weather. It's a nice place to people watch or catch up with a friend. With all the open windows, Reggie's definitely gives off a comfortable and homey vibe. I saw many patrons trickling in and greeting Reggie, something that is awesome to see as it shows he really cares about his customers.

They do have a happy hour gelato deal if I remember correctly. They're located next to Brite Spot Diner and a few blocks away from Echo Park. There's plenty of street parking if you don't mind walking a few minutes. Credit cards are also accepted!</text>< pics>

I‚Äôve been to La Buvette four times. Each time has been better than the last. The food and the wine (oh, the wine!) are excellent. The energy in the room is fantastic. The decor is stylishly done, very French neighborhood bistro without  anything overt or cliched. The owners are pros who bring no small amount of much-needed cachet to the area. The menu isn‚Äôt enormous, but it is thoughtfully done, so that anyone can find a choice of things to order. The wine list is impeccable. The charcuterie board is divine and the tomato tart is lovely. Every seafood item we‚Äôve ordered has been cooked perfectly and presented artfully. This place is everything a neighborhood bistro should be. It‚Äôs the hot spot in town. Go. You will be glad you did.< /Review>

Mona Telega< /name>
<date>1560131993174< /date><Rate>5</Rate>< review>
A true French bistro in San Pedro!  Everything is made in house with flair - from the baguette slices with le pettit beurre au sel, to the fragrant onion soup and mousse au chocolat. Paired with just the right wines - a rose for a warm summer night is spot on. Delightful French owners and wait staff caringly make you feel home. The decor is soothing, the skylights infuse the place with soft, natural light and, for a moment, looking at the ambient reflection in the patina-ed mirrors you feel you may be in Paris or on the Croisette, while Edith Piaf sounds gently through the place.   Repeat visits are a must...!< /review>

Between the end-of-year and holiday incentives, the dealer discounts, the ease of submitting an offer for a vehicle in the online inventory, and the near-immediate response by a member of the sales staff, there is no reason not to consider Fahrney Ford if you are looking to add to your rolling stock.
